<Text>April 1997: So, this review is a little belated, but look past that for a moment. Was cleaning out a closet at the house my parents lived in since 1982. <date>1479937588579</date><text>Pros and Cons of the Cesar's Way Fundamentals Class:
Pros: it's a super fun and entertaining class, you get a free leash and a free bag

Cons: -It's no longer taught by Brian Agnew and Cheri Lucas unfortunately.
-the class is huuuuge with over 30 people and 30 dogs. it costs $6000 which is insanely high.
-You only get to meet Cesar on the morning pack walk for about 3 minutes and he seems like he would rather be sleeping than walking with you and talking to you about your dog.
-there are so many dogs in the class that your dog might not get picked for any demonstrations or activities
-almost all dogs are so well behaved that they really don't need any corrections. (I was expecting red-zone dogs that you can really learn from)
-all your trainer conversations are with 6 to 8 different trainers (some paid some volunteers) who have totally different answers to the same question, leaving you more confused than ever
-if you watch every single episode of the Dog Whisperer, you will get the same information that's presented in the class.
-the whole experience feels very 'cult"-ish
In summary; if you are a person with limited finances, I think you are better off paying $6000 to either Cheri or Brian to rehabilitate you and your dog. Your dog will appreciate it more. The calamari was really good and so where the blistered peppers. The beers were inventive, but nothing blew my mind. The cherry hard seltzer was nice. < Review>
They're finally open!  Tried a flight of beers, and all of them were delicious.  Highly recommend this place if you're a big beer drinker.  I will be back many times!  The sour blackerry beer was great, check it out.  It has a very crisp aftertaste, and even those who aren't beer drinkers may like that one.

Mushroom pizza was delicious as well.  They used good quality mushrooms, and the crust was nice and chewy, but not too thick.  Pizza was a bit on the pricey side for $18/$19 for its size.  But it's clear that they used quality ingredients.

Service was a bit slow, it took a while to get our check.  Our server Lizz apologized.  She seemed a bit overwhelmed with the size of the crowd.  I think she was the only one taking orders that night.  Its clear they're still sorting things out, hence the soft opening.  Regardless, beer and food was great so I will be back!< /Review>
